                                        e.preventDefault();
                                        var t = $("#site-search__field").val().trim();
                                        if (t !== "") {

                    iconCodeMap.push({'iconCode' : '111', 'wiIcon' : 'wi-night-alt-sleet', 'lwiIcon' : 'lwi-night-alt-sleet'});
                    iconCodeMap.push({'iconCode' : '112', 'wiIcon' : 'wi-night-alt-sleet', 'lwiIcon' : 'lwi-night-alt-sleet'});
                    iconCodeMap.push({'iconCode' : '114', 'wiIcon' : 'wi-night-alt-snow', 'lwiIcon' : 'lwi-night-alt-snow'});
                    iconCodeMap.push({'iconCode' : '116', 'wiIcon' : 'wi-night-alt-thunderstorm', 'lwiIcon' : 'lwi-night-alt-thunderstorm'});
        
        function getWIIcon(iconCode) {
            for (var i =  0; i &lt; iconCodeMap.length; i ++) {
                if (iconCode == iconCodeMap[i].iconCode) {
                    if (iconSet != '#1') {
                        return iconCodeMap[i].lwiIcon;
                    } else {
                        return iconCodeMap[i].wiIcon;
                    }
                    
                }
            }
        }
        
        function getFullWI(iconCode, size) {
            if (iconSet != '#1') {
                return 'lwi ' + getWIIcon(iconCode) + ' ' + size;
            } else {
                return 'wi ' + getWIIcon(iconCode);
            }
        }

        function getIconStyle(size){
            var iconStyle = "";
            if (iconSet == 'custom') {
                if(size == 'large') {
                                        iconStyle = '';
                } else if(size == 'small') {
                                        iconStyle = '';
                } else {
                                        iconStyle = '';
                }
                return "background-image: url(" + iconStyle + ");";
             }
        }
        
        function showNoResult() {
            noResult.show();
            $('#right-now-' + articleId).hide();
            $('#details-' + articleId).hide();
            tonightEL.hide();
            dailyEl.hide();
        }
        
        function showResult() {
            noResult.hide();
            $('#right-now-' + articleId).show();
            $('#details-' + articleId).show();
            if (displayTonight) {
            	tonightEL.show();
            }
            if (displayDaily) {
        	    dailyEl.show();
        	}
        }
		
		function getTimeZoneOffset(hourlyForecast) {
			return new Date(hourlyForecast.validDateLocal).getTime() - new Date(hourlyForecast.validDateUtc).getTime();
		}
		
		function getCurrentLocalTime(hourlyForecast) {
		    var timeZoneOffset = getTimeZoneOffset(hourlyForecast);
			var currentDate = new Date($.ajax({async: false}).getResponseHeader("Date"));
			var currentTime = currentDate.getTime();
			var offset=currentDate.getTimezoneOffset()*60000;
			var localTime = currentTime + offset + timeZoneOffset;
			var currentLocalTime = new Date(localTime);
			return currentLocalTime;
		}
		
		function getTonightWeather(dailyForcastVOList, hourlyForcastVOList, currentLocalTime) {
		    var tonightWeather = {};
			var weekList = ["Sunday", "Monday", "Tuesday", "Wednesday", "Thursday", "Friday", "Saturday"];
			var todayDate = new Date(currentLocalTime.getFullYear(), currentLocalTime.getMonth(), currentLocalTime.getDate());
			var todayDayOfWeek = weekList[todayDate.getDay()];
			var tonightDate = new Date(currentLocalTime.getFullYear(), currentLocalTime.getMonth(), currentLocalTime.getDate(), 19);
			for (var i = 0; i &lt; hourlyForcastVOList.length; i++) {
				var hourlyWeather = hourlyForcastVOList[i];
				var validDateLocalDate = new Date(hourlyWeather.validDateLocal)
				if (validDateLocalDate &gt; currentLocalTime) {
					if (validDateLocalDate &gt;= tonightDate) {
						tonightWeather.hourlyWeatherTonight = hourlyWeather;
						break;
					}
				}
				
			}
			
			for (var i = 0; i &lt; dailyForcastVOList.length; i++) {
				var dailyWeather = dailyForcastVOList[i];
				if (todayDayOfWeek == dailyWeather.dayOfWk) {
					tonightWeather.todayWeather = dailyWeather;
					break;
				}
				
			}
			
			return tonightWeather;
		}
        
        $(searchBtn).click(function() {
            var zipCode = $('#weather-search-' + articleId).val().trim();
            var params = {				 
                'zipCode': zipCode,
                'groupId': '7636821',
                'companyId': '7631288',
            };
            var requestUrl = "/ep-wcm-portlet/restful/weatherSearch/searchWeatherByZipCode?" + $.param(params);
            
            $.ajax({
                type : "GET",
                url : requestUrl
            }).done(function(html) {
                var weatherForecastList = $(html);
                
                if (getDataFailed.is(':visible')) {
                    getDataFailed.hide();
                }
                
                if (weatherForecastList &amp;&amp; weatherForecastList.length &gt; 0) {
                    var currentConditionForecastVOList = weatherForecastList.get(0).CURRENT_CONDITION_FORECAST;
                    var dailyForcastVOList = weatherForecastList.get(0).DAILY_FORECAST;
                    var hourlyForcastVOList = weatherForecastList.get(0).HOURLY_FORECAST;
                    
                    // Current Condition
                    if (currentConditionForecastVOList &amp;&amp; currentConditionForecastVOList.length &gt; 0) {
                        var currentCondition = currentConditionForecastVOList[0];
                        var iconCode = currentCondition.iconCode;
                        var name = currentCondition.name;
                        var stateAbbr = currentCondition.stateAbbr;
                        var preferredZipCode = currentCondition.preferredZipCode;
						var currentZipCode = currentCondition.currentZipCode;
                        var wiIcon = getWIIcon(iconCode);
                        var tempF = currentCondition.tempF;
                        var sky = currentCondition.sky;
                        var feelsLikeF = currentCondition.feelsLikeF;
                        var wndSpdMph = currentCondition.wndSpdMph;
                        var wndDirCardinal = currentCondition.wndDirCardinal;
                        var relHumidity = currentCondition.relHumidity;
                        var dewPtF = currentCondition.dewPtF;
                        var pressure = currentCondition.pressure;
                        var sunrise = currentCondition.sunrise;
                        var sunset = currentCondition.sunset;
                        
                        showResult();
                        
                        if (iconCodeField &amp;&amp; wiIcon) {
                            iconCodeField.attr('class', getFullWI(iconCode, 'large'));
                            iconCodeField.attr('style', getIconStyle('large'));
                        }
                        if (locationField) {
                            locationField.text(name + ', ' + stateAbbr + ' ' + currentZipCode);
                        }
                        if (tempFField) {
                            tempFField.html(tempF + '&deg;F');
                        }
                                                if (skyField) {
                            skyField.html(sky);
                        }
                                                    skyField.append('&lt;span class="feels-like"&gt;Feels like ' + feelsLikeF + '&deg;&lt;/span&gt;');
                                                if (wndSpdDirField) {
                            wndSpdDirField.text(wndSpdMph + ' mph ' + wndDirCardinal);
                        }
                        if (relHumidityField) {
                            relHumidityField.text(relHumidity + '%');
                        }
                        if (dewPtFField) {
                            dewPtFField.html(dewPtF + '&deg;');
                        }
                        if (pressureField) {
                            pressureField.text(pressure + ' in');
                        }
                        if (sunriseField) {
                            sunriseField.text(sunrise + ' AM');
                        }
                        if (sunsetField) {
                            sunsetField.text(sunset + ' PM');
                        }
                    } else {
                        showNoResult();
                    }
                    
                    
                    if (dailyForcastVOList &amp;&amp; dailyForcastVOList.length &gt; 0) {
                        var todayEntry = dailyForcastVOList[0];
                        var dailyForcastItems = $('#daily-forcast-' + articleId +' &gt; li');
                        var temperature = tonightEL.find('.Temperature');
                        var details = tonightEL.find('.details');
                        
                        // Daily
                        dailyForcastItems.each(function(i) {
                            var dailyForcast = dailyForcastVOList[i];
                            
                            $(this).find('.day').text(dailyForcast.dayOfWk);
                            if ($(this).find('.temperature')) {
                                $(this).find('.temperature &gt; .high').html(dailyForcast.hiTempF + '&deg;');
                                $(this).find('.temperature &gt; .low').html(dailyForcast.loTempF + '&deg;');
                            }
                            if ($(this).find('.weather-icon')) {
                                var iconCode = dailyForcast.iconCode;
                                var wiIcon = getWIIcon(iconCode);
                                
                                $(this).find('.weather-icon &gt; i').attr('class', getFullWI(iconCode, 'medium'));
                                $(this).find('.weather-icon &gt; i').attr('style', getIconStyle('medium'));
                            }
                        });
                        
                        
                        
                    }
					// Tonight
					if (hourlyForcastVOList &amp;&amp; hourlyForcastVOList.length &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; dailyForcastVOList &amp;&amp; dailyForcastVOList.length &gt; 0) {
						var currentLocalTime = getCurrentLocalTime(hourlyForcastVOList[0])
						var tonightWeather = getTonightWeather(dailyForcastVOList, hourlyForcastVOList, currentLocalTime);
						if (tonightWeather.todayWeather &amp;&amp; tonightWeather.hourlyWeatherTonight) {
	                        var temperature = tonightEL.find('.temperature');
							                            var iconCodeNight = tonightWeather.hourlyWeatherTonight.iconCode;
                            var wiIconNight = getWIIcon(iconCodeNight);
                            
                            temperature.find('.weather-icon &gt; i').attr('class', getFullWI(iconCodeNight, 'medium'));
                            temperature.find('.weather-icon &gt; i').attr('style', getIconStyle('medium'));
	                        	                        	                            temperature.find('div').html(tonightWeather.todayWeather.loTempF + '&deg;F');
	                        	                        	                            temperature.find('.conditions').html(tonightWeather.hourlyWeatherTonight.skyLong);
	                        	                        	                            details.find('.wind &gt; .data').html(tonightWeather.hourlyWeatherTonight.wndSpdMph + ' mph ' + tonightWeather.hourlyWeatherTonight.wndDirCardinal);
	                        	                        
	                        details.find('.precip &gt; .data').html(tonightWeather.hourlyWeatherTonight.precipChance + '%');
	                        
	                        	                            details.find('.sunset &gt; .data').html(tonightWeather.todayWeather.sunset + ' PM');
	                        							
							if (sunriseField) {
	                            sunriseField.text(tonightWeather.todayWeather.sunrise + ' AM');
	                        }
	                        if (sunsetField) {
	                            sunsetField.text(tonightWeather.todayWeather.sunset + ' PM');
	                        }
	                        if (displayTonight) {
	                        	tonightEL.parent().parent().removeClass('no-later');
	                    	}
						} else {
							tonightEL.parent().parent().addClass('no-later');
						}
					} else {
						tonightEL.parent().parent().addClass('no-later');
					}
                }
            }).fail(function() {
                getDataFailed.show();
                console.log("Get current weather condition by zip code failed.");
            });
        });

		$(document).keydown(function (event) {
		    if (event.keyCode == 13 &amp;&amp; $("#weather-search-" + articleId).is(":focus")) {
		    	searchBtn.click();
		    }
		});
    })(jQuery);
/*]]&gt;*/
         </script>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
    </div>

        var autoflowId = $(this).children("option:selected").val();
        var ajaxUrl = $(this).attr("ajaxUrl");
		var tmpLimit = $(this).children("option:selected").attr("data-limit-number");
        var url = ajaxUrl + autoflowId;
		url = url.replace(/tmpLimitNum/, tmpLimit);
                var content = $("#content-mod-filtered-story-list-47026992");
        content.empty();
        content.append("&lt;div class='loader'&gt;&lt;img src='http://www.wfmz.com/wfmz-main-theme/images/loader.gif' alt='Loading'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;");

            type : "GET",
            url : url
        }).done(function(html) {
            var contentHTML = $(html);

        }).fail(function() {

         <script>
          /*&lt;![CDATA[*/
(function($, A){
    var loadMore = $('#load-more-mod-infinite-scrolling-media-headline-list-51311885');
    var alink = loadMore.children('a'); 
    alink.click(function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var ajaxUrl = alink.attr("ajaxUrl");
        var pageNum = parseInt(loadMore.attr("pageNum"));
        var autoflowId = loadMore.attr("autoflowId");
        if (false) {
            autoflowId = parseInt($("#filter-mod-infinite-scrolling-media-headline-list-51311885").val());
        }
                if(alink.hasClass("disabled")) {
            return;
        }
        $('#content-mod-infinite-scrolling-media-headline-list-51311885').append("&lt;div class='loader'&gt;&lt;img src='http://www.wfmz.com/wfmz-main-theme/images/loader.gif' alt='Loading'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;");
        alink.addClass("disabled");
        if (isNaN(pageNum)) {
            return;
        }
        var url = ajaxUrl + "autoflowId=" + autoflowId + "&pageNum;=" + pageNum;
        if (false) {
            var tmpLimit = $("#filter-mod-infinite-scrolling-media-headline-list-51311885").find("option:selected").attr("data-limit-number");
            url = url.replace(url.substring(url.indexOf("tmpLimit"), url.indexOf("&amp;", url.indexOf("tmpLimit"))), "tmpLimit=" + tmpLimit);
        }
        $.ajax({
            type : "GET",
            url : url
        }).done(function(html) {
            pageNum++;;
            loadMore.attr("pageNum", pageNum);
            var contentHTML = $(html).filter("ul");
            var stories = $('#content-mod-infinite-scrolling-media-headline-list-51311885').children('ul').first();
            var isViewList = stories.hasClass("view-list");
            if (isViewList) {
                if ("grid1" == "grid1") {
                    contentHTML.addClass("list media show-inline-ad small-block-grid-1 medium-block-grid-2 large-block-grid-3 view-list");
                } else if ("grid1" == "grid2") {
                    contentHTML.addClass("list media bricks view-list");
                }
            } else {
                if ("grid1" == "grid1") {
                    contentHTML.addClass("list media show-inline-ad small-block-grid-1 medium-block-grid-2 large-block-grid-3 view-grid");
                } else if ("grid1" == "grid2") {
                    contentHTML.addClass("list media bricks view-grid");
                }
            }
            $('#content-mod-infinite-scrolling-media-headline-list-51311885 .loader').remove();
            $("#content-mod-infinite-scrolling-media-headline-list-51311885").append(contentHTML);
            alink.removeClass("disabled");
        }).fail(function() {
            $("#content-mod-infinite-scrolling-media-headline-list-51311885").append("&lt;p class="text-center"&gt;Oops. Something went wrong. Please wait a minute and refresh your browser.&lt;/p&gt;")
        });
    });
    $("#filter-mod-infinite-scrolling-media-headline-list-51311885").change(function(){
        var loadMore = $('#load-more-mod-infinite-scrolling-media-headline-list-51311885');
        loadMore.attr("pageNum", 2);
        var autoflowId = $(this).children("option:selected").val();
        loadMore.attr("autoflowId", autoflowId);
        var ajaxUrl = $(this).attr("ajaxUrl");
        var tmpLimit = $(this).children("option:selected").attr("data-limit-number");
        var url = ajaxUrl + autoflowId;
        url = url.replace(/tmpLimitNum/, tmpLimit);
                loadMore.hide();
        loadMore.children('a').removeClass("disabled");
        var content = $("#content-mod-infinite-scrolling-media-headline-list-51311885");
        content.empty();
        content.append("&lt;div class="loader"&gt;&lt;img src="http://www.wfmz.com/wfmz-main-theme/images/loader.gif" alt="Loading"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;");
        $.ajax({
            type : "GET",
            url : url
        }).done(function(html) {
            var contentHTML = $(html).filter("ul");
            var isViewList = content.children('ul').first().hasClass("view-list");
            content.empty();
            if (isViewList) {
                if ("grid1" == "grid1") {
                    contentHTML.addClass("list media show-inline-ad small-block-grid-1 medium-block-grid-2 large-block-grid-3 view-list");
                } else if ("grid1" == "grid2") {
                    contentHTML.addClass("list media bricks view-list");
                }
            } else {
                if ("grid1" == "grid1") {
                    contentHTML.addClass("list media show-inline-ad small-block-grid-1 medium-block-grid-2 large-block-grid-3 view-grid");
                } else if ("grid1" == "grid2") {
                    contentHTML.addClass("list media bricks view-grid");
                }
            }
            content.append(contentHTML);
            loadMore.show();
        }).fail(function() {
            content.append("&lt;p class="text-center"&gt;Oops. Something went wrong. Please wait a minute and refresh your browser.&lt;/p&gt;")
        });
    });
})(jQuery, AUI());
/*]]&gt;*/
         </script>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>

            url : url

        }).fail(function() {
